(Modal):\n  ```php\n  add_filter('spectra_uagb/modal_blockdata', [$self, 'filter_modal_block_data']);\n  add_filter('spectra_modal_attributes', [$self, 'add_attributes_defaults']);\n Overrides**\n- `/blocks-config/freemium-blocks/*/block.php` extend free blocks\n- Uses filter system: `spectra_{block}_*` naming convention\n- Attributes merged via `array_merge()`\n\n**Method 3: Extension Loading**\n- `/core/extensions-manager.php` lazy-loads extensions:\n  - DynamicContent\n  - PopupBuilder\n  - QueryLoop\n  \n**Method 4: Render Block Filters**\n- Priority 11+ to avoid
